Mutungamiri MDC, VaMorgan Tsvangirai, vanoti vatsigiri vebato ravo vanofanirwa kuziva kuti zviuya zviri pemberi vobvisa Zanu PF kuburikidza nekuvhotera MDC-T zvine mutsindo musarudzo dza 2018. VaTsvangirai vakaudza vatsigiri vavo kuMakoni West nezuro kuti vanosungirwa kuramba vakabatana vachizonovhota vakawanda kuitira kudzivirira kubiridzirwa kunoitwa neZanu PF munguva yesarudzo. No media source currently available VaTsvangirai vakati vatsigiri vavo vanofanirwa kunyoresa kunovhota nguva dzose. Vakatiwo kana bato ravo richiita misangano, vatsigiri vanofanirwa kuenda kumisangano iyi nevana vavo vasvitsa makore ekuti vanenge vave kukodzera kuzovhota. VaTsvangirai vakati zvakavakoshera sebato kuti varwire kodzero dzevanhu vose munyika kuitira kupedza matambudziko akatarisana neveruzhinji anosanganisira kushayikwa kwemabasa, chikafu uye hurwere. Mutungamiriri weMDC akatiwo vaya vanoti vanhu vasina kurwira rusununguko rweZimbabwe havafanirwe kutonga nyika, vari kudivi rakashata renhoroondo yenyika. VaTsvangirai vakati hurumende yeZanu PF yakundikana kuwanira vanhu mabasa mamiriyoni maviri sekuvimbisa kwayakaita panguva yesarudzo asi avinoshamisa kuti yakwanisa kupedza kwemabasa kuvanhu mamiriyoni maviri kuburikidza nekuvhara kuri kuita makambani. VaTsvangirai vakati nzara iri muvanhu iri kuburitsa kutadza kutonga kwehurumende yeZanu PF, iyo vanoti haina mazano ekupedza nzara yakatarisana neruzhinji munyika. VaTsvangirai vakati rwendobato ravo richakwikwidza musarudzo dzemuna 2018, asi panguva imwe cheteyo vachiramba vakaomesa musoro kuti kutange kwave nekuvandudzwa kwemitemo ine chekuita nesarudzo.

Munyori mukuru weRANL — Moses Gukumure — anoti kugara nguva ndefu vatambi vasingatambe mutambo uyu, zvichikonzereswa nedenda reCovid-19, kwakadzosera kumashure kusimukira kwavo asi vave nemufaro zvichitevera kudzoka kwawakaita. “Mushure mekunge tapedza nguva ndefu mutambo uyu usiri kutambwa, zvinofadza zvikuru kuti tave kukwanisa kudzokera kuhupenyu hwedu hwekare vasikana vachitamba mutambo uyu unovararamisa. “Mutambo weDry Run wange uri wekuona kuti zvikwata zvave papi mugadziriro yekudzoka kwemutambo uyu. Tazvionera tega kuti zvagadzirira saka isu tagadzirirawo kuti mitambo ichitanga,” anodaro Gukumure. Zvisinei, anoti vachiri kumbomirira kupihwa mvumo kubva kuZimbabwe Netball Association (ZINA) neSports and Recreation Commission (SRC) kuti vachitanga mutambo uyu. Anoti kusvika pari zvino vanyorera kuZINA kanokwana katanhatu asi havasati vapihwa mhinduro. “Chiri kungotimisa kuti mitambo yedu ichitange kupihwa mvumo uye tinyoreswe neZINA. Takavanyorera asi havasati vatipindura kusvika pari zvino. Saka tiri kuramba tichigogodza kwavari, tichivanyorera kuti vatipe mvumo titange mitambo yedu,” anodaro. Zvichitevera kuvambwa kwakaitwawo ligi rePremier Netball League (PNL) nguva yadarika izvo zvakaona zvimwe zvikwata zvichibuda muRANL zvichienda kuPNL, Gukumure anoti maligi akawanda zvinobatsira kukura kwemutambo uyu uye zvichipa vatambi mikana yakasiyana yekukwikwidza. “Tichiri nezvikwata zvedu zvakawanda zvikuru uye isu tinovimba kuti zvapave nemaligi maviri zvichabatsira kukura kwemutambo uyu,” anodaro. Zvakadaro, chikwata cheZRP icho chakahwina mutambo uyu chakaenda kumba neUS$1 350 kuchiti zvimwe zvakakwikwidza zvinosanganisira Lusumbami, Tenax, Ruwa, Correctional Queens neKhami Prisons.

'''Kombiyuta''' (ku [[Chingezi]]: computer) imhando ye [[muchina]] unoshandisa zvemagetsi kuti chiyamuro, muitiro, chitoro, uye goho Dhata. Dhata iruzivo senge nhamba, mazwi, uye zvinyorwa. Input yedata zvinoreva kuverenga ruzivo kubva kubhodhi, mudziyo wekuchengetedza senge hard drive , kana sensor . Iyo komputa inochinja kana kushandura iyo data nekutevera iwo mirairo mune mapurogiramu esoftware. Iyo komputa chirongwa irondedzero yemirairidzo iyo komputa inofanirwa kuita. Zvirongwa zvinowanzoita masvomhu kuverenga, kugadzirisa data, kana kuifambisa. Iyo data inozochengetwa mumudziyo wekuchengetedza, unoratidzwa pachiratidziro, kana kutumirwa kune imwe komputa. Computers zvinogona kwakabatana pamwechete kuumba samambure yakadai internet , kubvumira makombiyuta kutaura nemumwe.

Kuhwina makwikwi eTM Bonanza promotion kwababa nemwana ane makore mashanu kokonzeresa mutauro muChinhoyi vamwe vachiti vanoshandisa mushonga kuti vahwine. VaClifton Mandla nemwana wavo Clinton ane makore mashanu ndivo vakahwina mibairo mukuru yeTM Bonanza promotion yakaitwa muChinhoyi neMugovera. Clinton akahwina mubairo mukuru wemari inosvika zviuru gumi, baba vake avo vanogaro vachihwina mibairo pachitoro cheTM muChinhoyi vakahwina zviuru zvishanu zvemadhora. Vamwe vagari vemuChinhoyi vanoti VaMandla vanoshandisa mushonga wekuti vahwine kana kuti vanorotswa. Amai Sobangile Kamudyariwa mumwe wevanofunga kuti VaMandla vanoshandisa mushonga kuti vahwine. Amai Kamudyariwa vanoti chimwe chinoshamisa ndechekuti VaMandla vari kuhwina pamakwikwi echitoro chimwechete izvo vanofunga kuti pane chitsotsi chirikuitwa nevashandi veTM. Asi VaMandla vanoti hapana mushonga wavanoshandisa vachiti vanohwina nekuti vanopinda mumakwiwi ose anoitika muzvitoro. VaMandla vanoramba kuti vanohwina makwiwi anoitwa muchitoro cheTM chete vachiti vanohwina makwiwi emunezvimwe zvitoro. VaMandla vakambohwina mamwe madhora zviuru zvishanu mugore ra2016, gore rakapera vakahwina firiji mumakwiwi ekwaTM Bonanza promotion. Vanoti mari yavahwina vachaishandisa kuvaka imba panzvimbo yavakatenga mushure mukuhwina mari yekutanga uye vanoti vacharamba vachipinda mumakwikwi ekwaTM nemunezvimwe zvitoro. Kunyange hazvo mutemo unoona nezvekupinda mumakwikwi usingabvimire kuti vana vane makore ari pasi pegumi nemasere vapinde mumakwikwi, chitoro cheTM chakaiswa panguva yakaomwa sezvo vainge vasina kunyora kuti makwikwi aya ayipindwa nevanhu vane makore mangani. Mukuru anoona nezvekushambadzirwa muzvitoro zvekwaTM Muzvare Paida Moyo vanoti vakaona kukanganisa uku Clinton atohwina vakatya kusamupa mubairo wake sezvo vaizoendeswa kumatare. Muzvare Moyo vanoti zvekuhwinisa mwana mudiki hazvichaitika zvakare. Zvitoro zvakawanda zvave kuita makwiwi ekuwanisa mibairo kuti vanhu vatenge zvinhu zvakawanda nechinangwa chekuhwina mibairo.
